palavraschave mudanco climatico aquecimento global meio am biente ministerio publico litigancia climatico Abstract thi paper aims to discuss how Brazilian prosecutors may act in defense of healthy climate systir combating global Warming to so it initially provide an overview of the sciencer behind climate change discussing its Causes and consequence to human and natural systems in sequence the paper examines how Brazilian legal frameworkr supports The assertion that Brazilian Government must act on The field of climater chan ge puting in place Mitigation and adptation measures finally the paper examines how Prosecoturs may Act to Combat global Warming approaching strategies of Mitigation and adaptation in order to foster further action from public and private sector Keywords climate Rio grande sul politico nacional mudanco climatico acao 92 resumo presente artigo tratar responsabilidade civil dano associado mudanco climatico tanto perspectiva preventivo reparato ria inicialmente Propoe caracterizacao de esse dano cumulativo seguida analisar alternativa teorico termos imputacao r ponsabilidade fim indicar hipotes responsabilidade civil apoio desenvolvimento ambito direito ambiental poder ter aplicacao promissor justico brasileiro palavraschaver responsabilidade civil dano cumulativo litigio cli matico abstract the article deals with civil liability damages associated with climater change both in its preventive and reparativer perspective it starts with the Characterization of these damages cumulative damages and afterwards it analyz theoretical alternative in terms of Imputation it conclude with the indication of hypotheses in which civil liability supported by its development in the scope of environmental law can have promising application in Brazilian revisitar dar condicoes uso instrumento economico palavraschave mudanco climatico politico ambiental instrumento economico funcao promocional direito abstract in view of the importance and timeliness of the discussion on climate change it is necessary to understand critically which environmental policy instruments are Most Suitable mitigating The effects of climate change thi article aims to analyze The usar of economic instruments in thi Context to thi end it seeks to understand The his torical context of The Creation of national and international environmental law The re lationship between environmental law and economics and the instruments of Environ mental policy it specifically analyzes the clean development mechanism cdm The generator of emission reduction certificate carbon credits and the instruments of law n 121872009 and law n 141192021 it conclude that the subsystems of the environmental and economic law are interlinked and that greater Effectiveness state Must Adopt policie that are defined the purposes proposed and that are effi cient finally that the ordering theory must be Revisited to give conditions to The use of economic instruments Keywords climate change abstract thi study aims to providir brief explanation about The relevance of solid Waste ma nagement in the Context of climate change and consequently of the need effectiver Measures to reduce greenhousir ga Emissions in thi sector and contribute to meeting The international commitments and goals assumed by Brazil by presenting an overview of the Brazilian panoramar With Regard to The Generation and disposal of solid waste the intention is to demonstrate The urgency of integrated actions aimed at implemen ting the Principles objective and instruments of the national solidr waste policy law n 1230510 and on The importance of the public prosecutorsr office to achiever these results reading through the text give rise to number of Reflections on how these en vironmental strategies and public policie can contribute to tackling climater change and sustainable development Keywords solid waste climate changes reverse logistic politica nacional mudanco climatico acaar 228 metodo dedutivo aler uso tecnica referente categorio conceito operacional pesquisa bibliografico palavra chave mudanco climatico planejamento urbano ministerio publico abstract thi article aims to evaluate The Work of the public prosecutorsr office in relation to The interface generated by The formation of Urban centers and the Causes and effects of climate change and The role of planning the vulnerability of Urban centers especially informal one requir the public ministry to Act more dynamic multidisciplinary and supportive based not only on legal Knowledge but other area including The use of Geographic Information systems Gis from photographs and georeferenced descrip tions to vector maps thi article addresse the concern with the development of citie Linked to sustainability guideline in order to usar urban planning way to mitigate and adapt to The effects of climate change Keywords climate change urban planning public ministry politico nacional mudanco climatico acao 282 Brazilian pantanal and cerrar region have been felt and measured by experts Whose phenomenon Acts in the degradation of social and economic conditiom of life adapted to Less aggressive cycle Which is enhan ced by The disorderly and hungry anthropization of space reproduction of economic activitie without concern environmental sustainability primarily agropastoral the routinar artifice of the Responsible integrated view of the natural consequence Flora Wildlife and humans The set of socioenvironmental analyse on Deforestation and forest fir example include the imperative of studies on climate change the necessarily protective Reaction Which is expected from government institutionsr requir clear and commit ted discourse on The effects of climate change on social organization and its economic activitie Within Which The Brazilian public prosecutorsr office in the Exercise of its cons titutional activity thi intervention calls militant desirir that become consistent with the awareness of the Real and the duty to act truly contributing to The realization of environmental Rights and by mandatory extension of social economic and cultural rights in shortr human rights and transforming People and groups hav ing drawn up The theoretical Contribution indigenous participation was contextualizedr Within the united nations frameworkr convention on climate change unfccc
